            <h2 class="headline">Dies ist ein Viergewinnt für Golfer, ihr könnt es mit 2 oder 4 Teams/Spielern spielen.</h2>
            <div class="choosespeech">
                <a href="./sprachauswahl/uk.html">Englisch (UK)</a>
            </div>
            <div>
                <h2 class="rules">Regelwerk</h2>
                <ul>
                    <li>Es wird abwechselnd gespielt.</li>
                    <li>Setze den Stein auf das Feld, das du getroffen hast.</li>
                    <li>Getroffene Felder können nicht mehr in der Farbe wechseln <br> <b> Bitte selber drauf achten. "Work in Procress."</b></li>
                </ul>
            </div>
            <div>
                <h2 class="levels">Level</h2>
                <ul>
                    <li>Bronze: Die Meterzahl gilt.</li>
                    <li>Silber: Die Meterzahl und die Seitliche abweichung gelten.</li>
                    <li>Gold: Felder können nur nach vorheriger ansage gespielt werden.</li>
                    <li>Platin: Wie Gold, alles mit einem Schläger.</li>
                </ul>
            </div>
            <div>
                <h2 class="modi">Spielmodi</h2>
                <ul>
                    <li><a href="../sprachen/de/html/Teams/2teams.html" class="link non-line">Zwei Spieler / Teams</a><small> -- Ist offline spielbar!</small></li>
                    <li><a href="../sprachen/de/html/Teams/2teams.html" class="link non-line">Drei Spieler / Teams</a><small> -- Ist nicht offline spielbar!</small></li>
                    <li><a href="../sprachen/de/html/Teams/2teams.html" class="link non-line">Vier Spieler / Teams</a><small> -- Ist nicht offline spielbar!</small></li>
                    <li><a href="../sprachen/de/html/Teams/2teams.html" class="link non-line">Fünf Spieler / Teams</a><small> -- Ist nicht offline spielbar!</small></li>
                    <li><a href="../sprachen/de/html/Teams/2teams.html" class="link non-line">Sechs Spieler / Teams</a><small> -- Ist nicht offline spielbar!</small></li>
                </ul>
            </div>
            <details open>
                <summary>Weiter Infos:</summary>
                <p id="indetails">Dieses Spiel ist für Golfer, die eine andere Art wollen zu trainiren,
                     Sie benötigen nur eine Art Trackman oder ein Simulator, um die exakte länge zuermitteln.
                    Nachdem sie die länge mit ihrem Trackman (o. ä.) ermittelt haben, können sie das mit dieser
                    länge beschriftet Feld in dem jeweiligen Spiel anklicken. Die Spiele wechseln Automatisch die Teams,
                    bzw. die Spieler durch. Viel Spaß beim spielen.
                </p>
                <a class="trackman" href="https://www.trackman.com/de">Hier könnten sie einen Trackman kaufen. (Sehr Teuer!)</a>

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta http-equiv="X-UA-Compatible" content="IE=edge">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Golf Four in a Row</title>
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="../style.css">
</head>
<body class="backgroundmain">
    <main>
        <div>
            <h2 class="headline">This is a four-in-a-row game for golfers, you can play it with 2/3/4/5/6 teams/players.</h2>
            <div class="choosespeech">
                <a href="../index.html">German</a>
            </div>
            <div>
                <h2 class="rules">Rules</h2>
                <ul>
                    <li>It will be played in turns.</li>
                    <li>Place the stone on the square you hit.</li>
                    <li>Fields that have been hit can no longer switch in the color <br>
                    <b> Please pay attention to it yourself. "Work in progress."</b></li>
                </ul>
            </div>
            <div>
                <h2 class="levels">Levels</h2>
                 <ul>
                     <li>Bronze: The number of meters applies.</li>
                     <li>Silver: The number of meters and the lateral deviation apply.</li>
                     <li>Gold: Fields can only be played after prior announcement.</li>
                     <li>Platinum: Like gold, all with a club.</li>
                 </ul>
            </div>
            <div>
                <h2 class="modi">Game modes</h2>
                 <ul>
                     <li><a href="../sprachen/uk/html/Teams/2teams.html" class="link non-line">Two players / teams</a><small> -- Can be played offline!</small></ li>
                     <li><a href="../sprachen/uk/html/Teams/3teams.html" class="link non-line">Three players / teams</a><small> -- Cannot be played offline!</small>< /li>
                     <li><a href="../sprachen/uk/html/Teams/4teams.html" class="link non-line">Four players / teams</a><small> -- Cannot be played offline!</small>< /li>
                     <li><a href="../sprachen/uk/html/Teams/5teams.html" class="link non-line">Five players / teams</a><small> -- Cannot be played offline!</small>< /li>
                     <li><a href="../sprachen/uk/html/Teams/6teams.html" class="link non-line">Six players / teams</a><small> -- Cannot be played offline!</small>< /li>
                 </ul>
            </div>
            <details open>
                <summary>More info:</summary>
                 <p id="indetails">This game is for golfers who want a different way to train,
                      You only need some kind of trackman or simulator to determine the exact length.
                     After you have determined the length with your Trackman (or similar), you can do this with this
                     Click on the field labeled length in the respective game. The games automatically switch teams,
                     or the players through. Have fun playing.
                 </p>
                 <a class="trackman" href="https://www.trackman.com/de">Here you could buy a Trackman. (Very expensive!)</a>
            </details>
        </div>
    </main>
</body>

    }

}

function changeTeam() {
    if (teams == 0) {
        teams = 1;
    } else if (teams == 1) {
        teams = 0;
    }
}

const infoElement = document.getElementById("info");

function hideInfo() {
    infoElement.style.display = "none";
}

function writeInfo(txt) {
    infoElement.style.display = "block";
    infoElement.innerHTML = txt;
}

function currentPlayer() {
    if(teams == 1) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team0;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: Das Dunkelgoldene Team ist dran!";
    }else if(teams == 0) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team1;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: Das Dunkelrote Team ist am Zug!";
    }else {
        console.log("Bitte Kontaktieren sie unseren Developer um im das Problem mit zu teilen! E-Mail: moinjulian.dev@outlook.com");
    }
}

function changeTeam() {
    if (teams == 0) {
        teams = 1;
    } else if (teams == 1) {
        teams = 2;
    } else if(teams == 2) {
        teams = 0
    }
}
  
const infoElement = document.getElementById("info");

function hideInfo() {
    infoElement.style.display = "none";
}

function writeInfo(txt) {
    infoElement.style.display = "block";
    infoElement.innerHTML = txt;
}

function currentPlayer() {
    if(teams == 0) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team1;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: Das Dunkelrote Team ist dran!";
    }else if(teams == 1) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team2;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: Das Dunkelblaue Team ist am Zug!";
    }else if(teams == 2) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team0;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: Das Dunkelgoldene Team ist dran!";
    }else {
        console.log("Bitte Kontaktieren sie unseren Developer um im das Problem mit zu teilen! E-Mail: moinjulian.dev@outlook.com");
    }
}

function TestWinBlue() {

        feld3 == team1 && feld10 == team1 && feld17 == team1 && feld24 == team1 ||
        feld10 == team1 && feld17 == team1 && feld24 == team1 && feld31 == team1 ||
        feld17 == team1 && feld24 == team1 && feld31 == team1 && feld38 == team1 ||
        feld24 == team1 && feld31 == team1 && feld38 == team1 && feld45 == team1 ||
        feld31 == team1 && feld38 == team1 && feld45 == team1 && feld52 == team1 ||
        //4. Spalte
        feld4 == team1 && feld11 == team1 && feld18 == team1 && feld25 == team1 ||
        feld11 == team1 && feld18 == team1 && feld25 == team1 && feld32 == team1 ||
        feld18 == team1 && feld25 == team1 && feld32 == team1 && feld39 == team1 ||
        feld25 == team1 && feld32 == team1 && feld39 == team1 && feld46 == team1 ||
        feld32 == team1 && feld39 == team1 && feld46 == team1 && feld53 == team1 ||
        //5. Spalte
        feld5 == team1 && feld12 == team1 && feld19 == team1 && feld26 == team1 ||
        feld12 == team1 && feld19 == team1 && feld26 == team1 && feld33 == team1 ||
        feld19 == team1 && feld26 == team1 && feld33 == team1 && feld40 == team1 ||
        feld26 == team1 && feld33 == team1 && feld40 == team1 && feld47 == team1 ||
        feld33 == team1 && feld40 == team1 && feld47 == team1 && feld54 == team1 ||
        //6. Spalte
        feld6 == team1 && feld13 == team1 && feld20 == team1 && feld27 == team1 ||

        feld20 == team1 && feld27 == team1 && feld34 == team1 && feld41 == team1 ||
        feld27 == team1 && feld34 == team1 && feld41 == team1 && feld48 == team1 ||
        feld34 == team1 && feld41 == team1 && feld48 == team1 && feld55 == team1 ||

        feld21 == team1 && feld28 == team1 && feld35 == team1 && feld42 == team1 ||
        feld28 == team1 && feld35 == team1 && feld42 == team1 && feld49 == team1 ||
        feld35 == team1 && feld42 == team1 && feld49 == team1 && feld56 == team1 
    ) {
        writeInfo("The Dark Red team won the game. <br> Congratulations!");
        setTimeout(function() {
            hideInfo();
            setNull();
        },2000)
    }
}

function changeTeam() {
    if (teams == 0) {
        teams = 1;
    } else if (teams == 1) {
        teams = 0;
    }
}

const infoElement = document.getElementById("info");

function hideInfo() {
    infoElement.style.display = "none";
}

function writeInfo(txt) {
    infoElement.style.display = "block";
    infoElement.innerHTML = txt;
}

function currentPlayer() {
    if(teams == 1) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team0;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: It's the Dark Gold team's turn!";
    }else if(teams == 0) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team1;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: It's the Dark Red Team's turn!";
    }else {
        console.log("Please contact our developer to let him know the problem! Email: moinjulian.dev@outlook.com");
    }
}

function changeTeam() {
    if (teams == 0) {
        teams = 1;
    } else if (teams == 1) {
        teams = 2;
    } else if(teams == 2) {
        teams = 0
    }
}
  
const infoElement = document.getElementById("info");

function hideInfo() {
    infoElement.style.display = "none";
}

function writeInfo(txt) {
    infoElement.style.display = "block";
    infoElement.innerHTML = txt;
}

function currentPlayer() {
    if(teams == 0) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team1;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: It's the Dark Red Team's turn!";
    }else if(teams == 1) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team2;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: It's the Dark Blue Team's turn!";
    }else if(teams == 2) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team0;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: It's the Dark Gold Team's turn!";
    }else {
        console.log("Please contact our developer to let him know the problem! Email: moinjulian.dev@outlook.com");
    }
}

function changeTeam() { //Wechselt das Team
    if (teams == 0) {
        teams = 1;
    } else if (teams == 1) {
        teams = 2;
    }else if(teams == 2) {
        teams = 3
    }else if(teams == 3) {
        teams = 0
    }
}
  
function currentPlayer() { //Druckt aus welches Team gerade dran ist.
    if(teams == 0) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team1;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: It's the Dark Red Team's turn!";
    }else if(teams == 1) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team2;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: It's the dark blue team's turn!";
    }else if(teams == 2) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team3;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: It's the dark orange team's turn!";
    }else if(teams == 3) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team0;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: It's the Dark Turquoise team's turn!";
    }else {
        console.log("Please contact our developer to let him know the problem! Email: moinjulian.dev@outlook.com");
    }
}

const infoElement = document.getElementById("info");

function hideInfo() {
    infoElement.style.display = "none";
}

function writeInfo(txt) {
    infoElement.style.display = "block";
    infoElement.innerHTML = txt;
}

function changeTeam() { //Wechselt das Team
    if (teams == 0) {
        teams = 1;
    } else if (teams == 1) {
        teams = 2;
    }else if(teams == 2) {
        teams = 3;
    }else if(teams == 3) {
        teams = 4;
    }else if(teams == 4) {
        teams = 0;
    }
}
  
function currentPlayer() { //Druckt aus welches Team gerade dran ist.
    if(teams == 0) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team1;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: It's the Dark Red Team's turn!";
    }else if(teams == 1) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team2;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: It's the Dark Blue Team's turn!";
    }else if(teams == 2) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team3;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: It's the dark orange team's turn!";
    }else if(teams == 3) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team4;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: It's the Dark Gray Team's turn!";
    }else if(teams == 4) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team0;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: It's the Dark Turquoise team's turn!";
    }else {
        console.log("Please contact our developer to let him know the problem! Email: moinjulian.dev@outlook.com");
    }
}

const infoElement = document.getElementById("info");

function hideInfo() {
    infoElement.style.display = "none";
}

function writeInfo(txt) {
    infoElement.style.display = "block";
    infoElement.innerHTML = txt;
}

function TestWinCyan() { //Testet ob das Türkise Team gewonnen hat.
    if (
        // 1. Reihe
        feld1 == team0 && feld2 == team0 && feld3 == team0 && feld4 == team0 ||
        feld2 == team0 && feld3 == team0 && feld4 == team0 && feld5 == team0 ||
        feld3 == team0 && feld4 == team0 && feld5 == team0 && feld6 == team0 ||
        feld4 == team0 && feld5 == team0 && feld6 == team0 && feld7 == team0 ||
        // 2. Reihe
        feld8 == team0 && feld9 == team0 && feld10 == team0 && feld11 == team0 ||
        feld9 == team0 && feld10 == team0 && feld11 == team0 && feld12 == team0 ||
        feld10 == team0 && feld11 == team0 && feld12 == team0 && feld13 == team0 ||
        feld11 == team0 && feld12 == team0 && feld13 == team0 && feld14 == team0 ||
        //3. Reihe
        feld15 == team0 && feld16 == team0 && feld17 == team0 && feld18 == team0 ||
        feld16 == team0 && feld17 == team0 && feld18 == team0 && feld19 == team0 ||
        feld17 == team0 && feld18 == team0 && feld19 == team0 && feld20 == team0 ||
        feld18 == team0 && feld19 == team0 && feld20 == team0 && feld21 == team0 ||
        //4.Reihe
        feld22 == team0 && feld23 == team0 && feld24 == team0 && feld25 == team0 ||
        feld23 == team0 && feld24 == team0 && feld25 == team0 && feld26 == team0 ||
        feld24 == team0 && feld25 == team0 && feld26 == team0 && feld27 == team0 ||
        feld25 == team0 && feld26 == team0 && feld27 == team0 && feld28 == team0 ||

        feld13 == team3 && feld20 == team3 && feld27 == team3 && feld34 == team3 ||
        feld20 == team3 && feld27 == team3 && feld34 == team3 && feld41 == team3 ||
        feld27 == team3 && feld34 == team3 && feld41 == team3 && feld48 == team3 ||
        feld34 == team3 && feld41 == team3 && feld48 == team3 && feld55 == team3 ||
        //7. Spalte
        feld7 == team3 && feld14 == team3 && feld21 == team3 && feld28 == team3 ||
        feld14 == team3 && feld21 == team3 && feld28 == team3 && feld35 == team3 ||
        feld21 == team3 && feld28 == team3 && feld35 == team3 && feld42 == team3 ||
        feld28 == team3 && feld35 == team3 && feld42 == team3 && feld49 == team3 ||
        feld35 == team3 && feld42 == team3 && feld49 == team3 && feld56 == team3 
    ) {
        writeInfo("Das Dunkelorangene Team hat das Spiel gewonnen. <br> Herzlichen Glückwunsch!");
        setTimeout(function() {
            location.reload();
        },2000)
    }
}

function changeTeam() { //Wechselt das Team
    if (teams == 0) {
        teams = 1;
    } else if (teams == 1) {
        teams = 2;
    }else if(teams == 2) {
        teams = 3
    }else if(teams == 3) {
        teams = 0
    }
}
  
function currentPlayer() { //Druckt aus welches Team gerade dran ist.
    if(teams == 0) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team1;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: Das Dunkelrote Team ist dran!";
    }else if(teams == 1) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team2;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: Das Dunkelblaue Team ist am Zug!";
    }else if(teams == 2) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team3;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: Das Dunkelorangene Team ist dran!";
    }else if(teams == 3) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team0;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: Das Dunkelgoldene Team ist dran!";
    }else {
        console.log("Bitte Kontaktieren sie unseren Developer um im das Problem mit zu teilen! E-Mail: moinjulian.dev@outlook.com");
    }
}

const infoElement = document.getElementById("info");

function hideInfo() {
    infoElement.style.display = "none";
}

function writeInfo(txt) {
    infoElement.style.display = "block";
    infoElement.innerHTML = txt;
}

function changeTeam() { //Wechselt das Team
    if (teams == 0) {
        teams = 1;
    } else if (teams == 1) {
        teams = 2;
    }else if(teams == 2) {
        teams = 3;
    }else if(teams == 3) {
        teams = 4;
    }else if(teams == 4) {
        teams = 5;
    }else if(teams = 5) {
        teams = 0;
    }
}
  
function currentPlayer() { //Druckt aus welches Team gerade dran ist.
    if(teams == 0) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team1;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: It's the Dark Red Team's turn!";
    }else if(teams == 1) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team2;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: It's the Dark Blue Team's turn!";
    }else if(teams == 2) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team3;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: It's the dark orange team's turn!";
    }else if(teams == 3) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team4;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: It's the Dark Gray Team's turn!";
    }else if(teams == 4) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team5;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: It's the Dark Turquoise team's turn!";
    }else if(teams == 5) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team0;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: It's the Dark Gold Team's turn!";
    }else {
        console.log("Please contact our developer to let him know the problem! Email: moinjulian.dev@outlook.com");
    }
}

const infoElement = document.getElementById("info");

function hideInfo() {
    infoElement.style.display = "none";
}

function writeInfo(txt) {
    infoElement.style.display = "block";
    infoElement.innerHTML = txt;
}

function changeTeam() { //Wechselt das Team
    if (teams == 0) {
        teams = 1;
    } else if (teams == 1) {
        teams = 2;
    }else if(teams == 2) {
        teams = 3;
    }else if(teams == 3) {
        teams = 4;
    }else if(teams == 4) {
        teams = 0;
    }
}
  
function currentPlayer() { //Druckt aus welches Team gerade dran ist.
    if(teams == 0) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team1;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: Das Dunkelrote Team ist dran!";
    }else if(teams == 1) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team2;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: Das Dunkelblaue Team ist am Zug!";
    }else if(teams == 2) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team3;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: Das Dunkelorangene Team ist dran!";
    }else if(teams == 3) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team4;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: Das Dunkelgraue Team ist dran!";
    }else if(teams == 4) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team0;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: Das Dunkelgoldene Team ist dran!";
    }else {
        console.log("Bitte Kontaktieren sie unseren Developer um im das Problem mit zu teilen! E-Mail: moinjulian.dev@outlook.com");
    }
}

const infoElement = document.getElementById("info");

function hideInfo() {
    infoElement.style.display = "none";
}

function writeInfo(txt) {
    infoElement.style.display = "block";
    infoElement.innerHTML = txt;
}

function TestWinGold() { //Testet ob das Türkise Team gewonnen hat.
    if (
        // 1. Reihe
        feld1 == team0 && feld2 == team0 && feld3 == team0 && feld4 == team0 ||
        feld2 == team0 && feld3 == team0 && feld4 == team0 && feld5 == team0 ||
        feld3 == team0 && feld4 == team0 && feld5 == team0 && feld6 == team0 ||
        feld4 == team0 && feld5 == team0 && feld6 == team0 && feld7 == team0 ||
        // 2. Reihe
        feld8 == team0 && feld9 == team0 && feld10 == team0 && feld11 == team0 ||
        feld9 == team0 && feld10 == team0 && feld11 == team0 && feld12 == team0 ||
        feld10 == team0 && feld11 == team0 && feld12 == team0 && feld13 == team0 ||
        feld11 == team0 && feld12 == team0 && feld13 == team0 && feld14 == team0 ||
        //3. Reihe
        feld15 == team0 && feld16 == team0 && feld17 == team0 && feld18 == team0 ||
        feld16 == team0 && feld17 == team0 && feld18 == team0 && feld19 == team0 ||
        feld17 == team0 && feld18 == team0 && feld19 == team0 && feld20 == team0 ||
        feld18 == team0 && feld19 == team0 && feld20 == team0 && feld21 == team0 ||
        //4.Reihe
        feld22 == team0 && feld23 == team0 && feld24 == team0 && feld25 == team0 ||
        feld23 == team0 && feld24 == team0 && feld25 == team0 && feld26 == team0 ||
        feld24 == team0 && feld25 == team0 && feld26 == team0 && feld27 == team0 ||
        feld25 == team0 && feld26 == team0 && feld27 == team0 && feld28 == team0 ||
        //5. Reihe
        feld29 == team0 && feld30 == team0 && feld31 == team0 && feld32 == team0 ||
        feld30 == team0 && feld31 == team0 && feld32 == team0 && feld33 == team0 ||
        feld31 == team0 && feld32 == team0 && feld33 == team0 && feld34 == team0 ||
        feld32 == team0 && feld33 == team0 && feld34 == team0 && feld35 == team0 ||
        //6. Reihe
        feld36 == team0 && feld37 == team0 && feld38 == team0 && feld39 == team0 ||
        feld37 == team0 && feld38 == team0 && feld39 == team0 && feld40 == team0 ||
        feld38 == team0 && feld39 == team0 && feld40 == team0 && feld41 == team0 ||
        feld39 == team0 && feld40 == team0 && feld41 == team0 && feld42 == team0 ||
        // 7. Reihe
        feld43 == team0 && feld44 == team0 && feld45 == team0 && feld46 == team0 ||
        feld44 == team0 && feld45 == team0 && feld46 == team0 && feld47 == team0 ||
        feld45 == team0 && feld46 == team0 && feld47 == team0 && feld48 == team0 ||
        feld46 == team0 && feld47 == team0 && feld48 == team0 && feld48 == team0 ||
        //8. Reihe

function changeTeam() { //Wechselt das Team
    if (teams == 0) {
        teams = 1;
    } else if (teams == 1) {
        teams = 2;
    }else if(teams == 2) {
        teams = 3;
    }else if(teams == 3) {
        teams = 4;
    }else if(teams == 4) {
        teams = 5;
    }else if(teams = 5) {
        teams = 0;
    }
}
  
function currentPlayer() { //Druckt aus welches Team gerade dran ist.
    if(teams == 0) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team1;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: Das Dunkelrote Team ist dran!";
    }else if(teams == 1) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team2;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: Das Dunkelblaue Team ist am Zug!";
    }else if(teams == 2) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team3;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: Das Dunkelorangene Team ist dran!";
    }else if(teams == 3) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team4;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: Das Dunkelgraue Team ist dran!";
    }else if(teams == 4) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team5;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: Das Dunkeltürkise Team ist dran!";
    }else if(teams == 5) {
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").style.backgroundColor = team0;
        document.getElementById("currentPlayer").innerHTML = "Team: Das Dunkelgoldene Team ist dran!";
    }else {
        console.log("Bitte Kontaktieren sie unseren Developer um im das Problem mit zu teilen! E-Mail: moinjulian.dev@outlook.com");
    }
}

const infoElement = document.getElementById("info");

function hideInfo() {
    infoElement.style.display = "none";
}

function writeInfo(txt) {
    infoElement.style.display = "block";
    infoElement.innerHTML = txt;
}
